      <script type="text/javascript">
       $(document).ready(function() {
             function changeElement(elem) {
                 if (elem.classList.contains('dark_font')) {
                     $('.cycle-cmd-button--pause')[0].style.color = "black";
                     $('.cycle-cmd-button--resume')[0].style.color = "black";
                     $('.cycle-overlay-pager li:not(.cycle-pager-active)').each(function() {
                         $(this)[0].style.color = "#AFAFAF";
                     });
                     $('.cycle-overlay-pager li.cycle-pager-active')[0].style.color = "black";
                 } else {
                     $('.cycle-cmd-button--pause')[0].style.color = "white";
                     $('.cycle-cmd-button--resume')[0].style.color = "white";
                     $('.cycle-overlay-pager li:not(.cycle-pager-active)').each(function() {
                         $(this)[0].style.color = "#AFAFAF";
                     });
                     $('.cycle-overlay-pager li.cycle-pager-active')[0].style.color = "white";
                 }
             }
 
             function changeFirstElement() {
                 if ($('.cycle-slideshow .slide .cycle-overlay.custom h2')[0].classList.contains('dark_font')) {
                     $('.cycle-cmd-button--pause')[0].style.color = "black";
                     $('.cycle-cmd-button--resume')[0].style.color = "black";
                     $('.cycle-pager li').each(function() {
                         $(this)[0].style.color = "#AFAFAF";
                     });
                     $('.cycle-pager li')[0].style.color = "black";
                 } else {
                     $('.cycle-pager li')[0].style.color = "white";
                 }
 
             }
 
             $('.cycle-slideshow').on('cycle-post-initialize', function(event, optionHash) {
                 changeFirstElement();
             });
 
             $('.cycle-slideshow').on('cycle-after', function(event, optionHash, outgoingSlideEl, incomingSlideEl, forwardFlag) {
                 if (incomingSlideEl.children[0].className != "cycle-overlay-mask") {
                     changeElement(incomingSlideEl.children[0].firstElementChild);
                 } else {
                     changeElement(incomingSlideEl.children[1].firstElementChild);
                 }
             });
         });
      </script>

      <script type="text/javascript">
       $(document).ready(function() {
         $.ajax({
             url: "/twitter/getfeed",
             type: 'GET',
             dataType: 'json',
             contentType: 'application/json; charset=utf-8',
             success: function(data) {
                 for (i = 0 ; i < data.length ; i++) {
                     $(".jcarousel-list").append("<p class=\"jcarousel-item\"><span>" + data[i] + "</span></p>")
                 }
                 $('.jcarousel').jcarousel({
                     list: '.jcarousel-list',
                     wrap: 'both',
                     vertical: true
                 }).jcarouselAutoscroll({
                     interval: 5000,
                     target: '+=1',
                     autostart: true
                 });
 
                 // Delete CSS class that append the external link image
                 $(".jcarousel-item a").each(function() { $(this).removeClass("link-button__link--external"); });
                 $(".twitter-link").removeClass("link-button__link--external");
 
                 // jCarousel Previous Tweet button control
                 $('.twitter-carousel__prev').jcarouselControl({
                     target: '-=1'
                 });
 
                 // jCarousel Next Tweet button control
                 $('.twitter-carousel__next').jcarouselControl({
                     target: '+=1'
                 });
 
                 // Define the new interval for jCarousel Autoscroll
                 $('.jcarousel').jcarouselAutoscroll({ interval: 5000 });
 
                 // Custom Pause Button for jCarousel Autoscroll
                 $('.twitter-carousel__pause').click(function() {
                     $(this).addClass('hidden');
                     $('.twitter-carousel__play').removeClass('hidden');
                     $('.jcarousel').jcarouselAutoscroll('stop');
                 });
 
                 // Custom Play Button for jCarousel Autoscroll
                 $('.twitter-carousel__play').click(function() {
                     $(this).addClass('hidden');
                     $('.twitter-carousel__pause').removeClass('hidden');
                     $('.jcarousel').jcarouselAutoscroll('start');
                 });
 
             }
         });
     });
      </script>

        <h2 class="home-thematic__title colored">
         <span class="home-thematic__title--text">
          Professionnels de la recherche
         </span>
        </h2>
        <article class="home-thematic__item">
         <h3 class="home-thematic__item__title">
          <a href="/Professionnels-de-sante/Veille-bibliographique/Nota-Bene-Cancer" id="link__home-thematic__item_96259">
           Nota Bene Cancer
          </a>
         </h3>
         <p class="home-thematic__item__text">
          Nota Bene Cancer permet à ses abonnés de gagner du temps pour se tenir informé de l’actualité scientifique et médicale dans les divers domaines de la recherche sur les cancers.
         </p>
         <a aria-describedby="link__home-thematic__item_96259" class="home-thematic__item__link colored" href="/Professionnels-de-sante/Veille-bibliographique/Nota-Bene-Cancer" rel="no-follow" title="Nota Bene Cancer (en savoir plus)">
          en savoir plus
         </a>
        </article>
        <article class="home-thematic__item">
         <h3 class="home-thematic__item__title">
          <a href="/Professionnels-de-la-recherche/Recherches-en-sante-des-populations/Recherche-interventionnelle" id="link__home-thematic__item_184459">
           La recherche interventionnelle
          </a>
         </h3>
         <p class="home-thematic__item__text">
          La recherche interventionnelle vise à tester, sur le terrain, des hypothèses touchant à tous les domaines de la recherche contre le cancer, depuis la prévention primaire jusqu’à l’après-cancer.
         </p>
         <a aria-describedby="link__home-thematic__item_184459" class="home-thematic__item__link colored" href="/Professionnels-de-la-recherche/Recherches-en-sante-des-populations/Recherche-interventionnelle" rel="no-follow" title="La recherche interventionnelle (en savoir plus)">
          en savoir plus
         </a>
        </article>
        <article class="home-thematic__item">
         <h3 class="home-thematic__item__title">
          <a href="/Professionnels-de-la-recherche/Recherche-translationnelle/Les-SIRIC" id="link__home-thematic__item_146377">
           Les SIRIC
          </a>
         </h3>
         <p class="home-thematic__item__text">
          Huit SIRIC réunissent, autour d'un même site, des services médicaux, des équipes de recherche multidisciplinaire et des ressources et services communs performants.
         </p>
         <a aria-describedby="link__home-thematic__item_146377" class="home-thematic__item__link colored" href="/Professionnels-de-la-recherche/Recherche-translationnelle/Les-SIRIC" rel="no-follow" title="Les SIRIC (en savoir plus)">
          en savoir plus
         </a>
        </article>
        <div class="push-image">
         <a class="push-image__content" href="/Institut-national-du-cancer/Appels-a-projets" target="_self">
          <span class="mask-opacity">
          </span>
          <img alt="" class="img-responsive" height="110" src="/var/inca/storage/images/ecancer/accueil/pushs-image-pour-la-homepage/appels-a-projets/1052759-1-fre-FR/Appels-a-projets_hp_bandeau3.png" style="border: 0px  ;" width="269"/>
          <span class="push-image__content__title">
           Appels à projets
          </span>
         </a>
        </div>
       </section>
      </div>
      <div class="row home-teaching-columns">
       <section class="home-teaching-column col-md-4 col-xs-12">
        <div class="row">
         <div class="col-xs-6 col-sm-12 col-md-6 home-teaching-column__vignette">
          <a class="push-image__content" href="/Dictionnaire/S/sevrage" target="_self">
           <div class="home-teaching__highlight">
            <span class="home-teaching__highlight--align typo--normal">
             Sevrage
            </span>
           </div>
          </a>
         </div>
         <div class="col-xs-6 col-sm-12 col-md-6">
          <div class="home-teaching__content">
           <h2 class="home-teaching__content__title">
            Le terme
           </h2>
           <div class="home-teaching__text-container">
            <p class="home-teaching__content__text">
             Action de ne plus consommer un produit tel que l’alcool, le tabac, etc.
            </p>
           </div>
           <a class="home-teaching__content__link marging-image-accueil" href="/Dictionnaire/A" target="_self">
            Dictionnaire
           </a>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
       </section>
       <section class="home-teaching-column col-md-4 col-xs-12">
        <div class="row">
         <div class="col-xs-6 col-sm-12 col-md-6 home-teaching-column__vignette">
          <a class="push-image__content" href="/Acces-thematique/Prevention-des-cancers" target="_self">
           <div class="home-teaching__highlight">
            <span class="home-teaching__highlight--align typo--bigger">
             40%
            </span>
           </div>
          </a>
         </div>
         <div class="col-xs-6 col-sm-12 col-md-6">
          <div class="home-teaching__content">
           <h2 class="home-teaching__content__title">
            Le chiffre
           </h2>
           <div class="home-teaching__text-container">
            <p class="home-teaching__content__text">
             C’est la part de cancers qui pourraient être évités en changeant nos comportement.
            </p>
           </div>
           <a class="home-teaching__content__link marging-image-accueil" href="/Comprendre-prevenir-depister/Se-faire-depister/Depistage-du-cancer-colorectal" target="_self">
